# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api`, `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd`

# Kubernetes Admission Webhook Processing Chain

## Your Task

Trace the admission webhook processing chain in Kubernetes. Find Go source files across kubernetes/kubernetes and kubernetes/api that implement: the generic Webhook dispatcher (in pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/), the mutating webhook dispatcher with reinvocation logic, the validating webhook dispatcher with parallel dispatch, the WebhookAccessor abstraction layer, and the MutatingWebhookConfiguration/ValidatingWebhookConfiguration API type definitions.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

48-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully traced the Kubernetes admission webhook processing chain and documented all findings in `/workspace/answer.json`. 

Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Components Identified:

1. **Generic Webhook Dispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/`)
   - `webhook.go`: Core `Webhook` struct managing the admission plugin infrastructure
   - `interfaces.go`: `Dispatcher`, `Source`, and `WebhookInvocation` interfaces

2. **WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`)
   - Unified interface for both mutating and validating webhooks
   - `mutatingWebhookAccessor` and `validatingWebhookAccessor` implementations
   - Factory functions: `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()`

3. **Mutating Webhook Dispatcher** with Reinvocation Logic
   - `dispatcher.go`: Sequential dispatch with `webhookReinvokeContext` for tracking reinvocation
   - `plugin.go`: `MutatingAdmissionWebhook` plugin implementation
   - Supports `IfNeededReinvocationPolicy` for reruns when objects mutate

4. **Validating Webhook Dispatcher** with Parallel Dispatch
   - `dispatcher.go`: Parallel execution using goroutines with `sync.WaitGroup`
   - `plugin.go`: `ValidatingAdmissionWebhook` plugin implementation
   - Implements panic recovery and independent failure policy handling

5. **Configuration Managers** 
   - `mutating_webhook_manager.go`: Watches and manages `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` objects
   - `validating_webhook_manager.go`: Watches and manages `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` objects

6. **API Type Definitions** (`github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api`)
   - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` and `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` in v1 and v1beta1

control:\\n\\n## Architecture Overview\\n\\nThe admission webhook processing chain in Kubernetes is implemented across multiple packages with a clear separation of concerns:\\n\\n### 1. Generic Webhook Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/)\\n\\nThe generic package provides the foundational webhook infrastructure:\\n\\n- **webhook.go**: Contains the `Webhook` struct that serves as the abstract admission plugin with infrastructure for both mutating and validating webhooks. The `NewWebhook()` function initializes webhooks with configuration management and dispatcher factories. The `Dispatch()` method coordinates webhook execution by fetching hooks from the source and delegating to the specific dispatcher.\\n\\n- **interfaces.go**: Defines critical interfaces:\\n  - `Dispatcher` interface: Implemented by both mutating and validating dispatchers, defines the `Dispatch()` method that processes admission requests\\n  - `Source` interface: Lists dynamic webhook plugins from configuration\\n  - `WebhookInvocation` struct: Encapsulates how to call a webhook with resource/kind information\\n  - `VersionedAttributeAccessor` interface: Manages versioned attributes for different API versions\\n\\n### 2. WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go)\\n\\nThe `WebhookAccessor` interface provides a common abstraction for both mutating and validating webhooks:\\n\\n- **WebhookAccessor interface**: Defines methods for accessing webhook properties (name, rules, failure policy, namespaceSelector, objectSelector, sideEffects, timeout, etc.) and retrieving RESTClient connections.\\n\\n- **mutatingWebhookAccessor**: Implements WebhookAccessor for v1.MutatingWebhook, provides cached access to REST clients and compiled CEL matchers\\n\\n- **validatingWebhookAccessor**: Implements WebhookAccessor for v1.ValidatingWebhook, similar to mutating but for validation scenarios\\n\\n- **Factory functions**: `NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()` and `NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()` create typed accessors with unique identifiers and configuration names\\n\\n### 3. Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/)\\n\\n- **dispatcher.go**: The `mutatingDispatcher` implements the `Dispatcher` interface and orchestrates mutating webhook execution with reinvocation support:\\n  - `Dispatch()` method handles the reinvocation context to support in-tree plugin reinvocation when object mutations occur\\n  - `webhookReinvokeContext` tracks which webhooks were invoked and whether reinvocation is needed\\n  - Supports `IfNeededReinvocationPolicy` for webhooks that need to be reinvoked when the object changes\\n  - Handles patching, mutation tracking, and audit annotations\\n  - Implements failure policy handling (Ignore or Fail)\\n\\n- **plugin.go**: The `Plugin` struct wraps `generic.Webhook` and implements `admission.MutationInterface`:\\n  - `NewMutatingWebhook()` creates the plugin with mutating-specific dispatcher\\n  - `Admit()` method calls `Webhook.Dispatch()` for admission checks\\n\\n### 4. Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/)\\n\\n- **dispatcher.go**: The `validatingDispatcher` implements the `Dispatcher` interface with parallel webhook execution:\\n  - `Dispatch()` method collects relevant hooks and spawns goroutines for parallel invocation\\n  - Uses `sync.WaitGroup` and channels to coordinate parallel webhook calls\\n  - Implements panic recovery for individual webhook failures\\n  - Supports failure policies independently for each webhook\\n  - Caches versioned attributes to avoid redundant conversions during parallel calls\\n\\n- **plugin.go**: The `Plugin` struct wraps `generic.Webhook` and implements `admission.ValidationInterface`:\\n  - `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates the plugin with validating-specific dispatcher\\n  - `Validate()` method calls `Webhook.Dispatch()` for validation checks\\n\\n### 5. Configuration Management\\n\\n- **mutating_webhook_manager.go** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/): \\n  - `mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source` interface\\n  - `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates manager that watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n  - Provides `Webhooks()` method that returns merged webhook accessors\\n  - Uses informer-based caching with lazy evaluation\\n\\n- **validating_webhook_manager.go** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/):\\n  - `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source` interface\\n  - `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates manager that watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n  - Provides `Webhooks()` method that returns merged webhook accessors\\n  - Uses same informer-based caching pattern as mutating manager\\n\\n### 6. API Type Definitions (github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api)\\n\\n- **admissionregistration/v1/types.go**:\\n  - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` struct: Top-level resource for configuring mutating admission webhooks\\n  - `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` struct: Top-level resource for configuring validating admission webhooks\\n  - `MutatingWebhook` struct: Individual webhook definition with rules, client config, and policies\\n  - `ValidatingWebhook` struct: Individual webhook definition for validation scenarios\\n  - Both webhook types support: rules matching, namespace/object selectors, failure policies, timeout settings, admission review versions, and match conditions\\n\\n- **admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go**: Deprecated versions maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\n## Processing Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Initialization**: `NewMutatingWebhook()` or `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates plugin instances that wrap `generic.Webhook`\\n\\n2. **Configuration Loading**: Configuration managers (`mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager`, `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager`) watch for MutatingWebhookConfiguration/ValidatingWebhookConfiguration changes via informers\\n\\n3. **Webhook Discovery**: `generic.Webhook.Dispatch()` fetches active webhooks from the configuration manager's `Webhooks()` method, which returns `WebhookAccessor` implementations\\n\\n4. **Matching**: For each webhook, `ShouldCallHook()` in generic.Webhook evaluates namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions using `WebhookAccessor` methods\\n\\n5. **Dispatch Decision**: Matching webhooks are passed to the specific dispatcher:\\n   - **Mutating**: Sequential execution with reinvocation logic, tracks mutations and reruns eligible webhooks\\n   - **Validating**: Parallel execution using goroutines, collects errors from all webhooks\\n\\n6. **Execution**: Dispatchers use `WebhookAccessor.GetRESTClient()` to establish connections and call remote webhooks\\n\\n7. **Result Handling**: Responses are processed according to failure policies and audit requirements\\n\\nThis architecture enables flexible, dynamic admission control with support for both sequential mutation tracking and parallel validation across multiple webhooks.\"\n}\n",

Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/)\\n\\n- **dispatcher.go**: The `validatingDispatcher` implements the `Dispatcher` interface with parallel webhook execution:\\n  - `Dispatch()` method collects relevant hooks and spawns goroutines for parallel invocation\\n  - Uses `sync.WaitGroup` and channels to coordinate parallel webhook calls\\n  - Implements panic recovery for individual webhook failures\\n  - Supports failure policies independently for each webhook\\n  - Caches versioned attributes to avoid redundant conversions during parallel calls\\n\\n- **plugin.go**: The `Plugin` struct wraps `generic.Webhook` and implements `admission.ValidationInterface`:\\n  - `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates the plugin with validating-specific dispatcher\\n  - `Validate()` method calls `Webhook.Dispatch()` for validation checks\\n\\n### 5. Configuration Management\\n\\n- **mutating_webhook_manager.go** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/): \\n  - `mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source` interface\\n  - `NewMutatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates manager that watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n  - Provides `Webhooks()` method that returns merged webhook accessors\\n  - Uses informer-based caching with lazy evaluation\\n\\n- **validating_webhook_manager.go** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/):\\n  - `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager` implements `generic.Source` interface\\n  - `NewValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager()` creates manager that watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n  - Provides `Webhooks()` method that returns merged webhook accessors\\n  - Uses same informer-based caching pattern as mutating manager\\n\\n### 6. API Type Definitions (github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api)\\n\\n- **admissionregistration/v1/types.go**:\\n  - `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` struct: Top-level resource for configuring mutating admission webhooks\\n  - `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` struct: Top-level resource for configuring validating admission webhooks\\n  - `MutatingWebhook` struct: Individual webhook definition with rules, client config, and policies\\n  - `ValidatingWebhook` struct: Individual webhook definition for validation scenarios\\n  - Both webhook types support: rules matching, namespace/object selectors, failure policies, timeout settings, admission review versions, and match conditions\\n\\n- **admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go**: Deprecated versions maintained for backward compatibility\\n\\n## Processing Chain Flow\\n\\n1. **Initialization**: `NewMutatingWebhook()` or `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates plugin instances that wrap `generic.Webhook`\\n\\n2. **Configuration Loading**: Configuration managers (`mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager`, `validatingWebhookConfigurationManager`) watch for MutatingWebhookConfiguration/ValidatingWebhookConfiguration changes via informers\\n\\n3. **Webhook Discovery**: `generic.Webhook.Dispatch()` fetches active webhooks from the configuration manager's `Webhooks()` method, which returns `WebhookAccessor` implementations\\n\\n4. **Matching**: For each webhook, `ShouldCallHook()` in generic.Webhook evaluates namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions using `WebhookAccessor` methods\\n\\n5. **Dispatch Decision**: Matching webhooks are passed to the specific dispatcher:\\n   - **Mutating**: Sequential execution with reinvocation logic, tracks mutations and reruns eligible webhooks\\n   - **Validating**: Parallel execution using goroutines, collects errors from all webhooks\\n\\n6. **Execution**: Dispatchers use `WebhookAccessor.GetRESTClient()` to establish connections and call remote webhooks\\n\\n7. **Result Handling**: Responses are processed according to failure policies and audit requirements\\n\\nThis architecture enables flexible, dynamic admission control with support for both sequential mutation tracking and parallel validation across multiple webhooks.\"\n}\n",
